data-ua-type="1" onclick="stpPgtnAndPrvntDefault(event)"><span>What made ZigZag Vodka a global winner at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025</span></h1></div><div class="t8vf3 byline_action"><div class="xf8Pm byline"><a href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/toireporter/author-toi-lifestyle-desk-479263437.cms" commonState="[object Object]" rel="noopener" frmappuse="1">TOI Lifestyle Desk</a> / etimes.in / <span>Updated: Sep 01, 2025, 09:32 IST</span></div><div class="eg6hg" data-socialshare="123569554"><div class="okf2Z"><div class="nSsMM "><div id="abound-123569554"       e3kx0
      
      
    "><a href="https://www.google.com/preferences/source?q=timesofindia.indiatimes" target="_blank" commonState="[object Object]" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer" frmappuse="1"><img src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/123518384.cms" alt="" imgsize="23456" resizemode="4" title="" offsetvertical="0" placeholdersrc="" placeholdermsid="" msid="" type="thumb" class=""/></a></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="clearfix"></div><div class="JuyWl CpKyX"><div class="vSlIC  "><div class="heightCalc"><div class="art_synopsis"><div data-type="in_view" class="  "><div class="tCKCr  id-r-synopsis"><div class="faiOF"><div class="WEwSo"><div class="M1rHh undefined" data-ua-type="1" onclick="stpPgtnAndPrvntDefault(event)">ZigZag Vodka, an Indian spirit, made a splash at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025, securing multiple silver and a bronze medal across its vodka variants. This achievement highlights the growing craftsmanship within India's spirits industry and the global interest in innovative vodka expressions.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-articlebody="1" class="fewcent-123569554 js_tbl_article"><div class="_s30J clearfix  "><div class="MwN2O"><div class="vdo_embedd"> <div class="T22zO"><section class="D3Wk1  clearfix id-r-component leadmedia undefined undefined  VtlfQ" style="top:0px"><div class="D3Wk1" data-ua-type="1" onclick="stpPgtnAndPrvntDefault(event)"><div class="zPaFh"><div class="wJnIp"><img src="https://static.toiimg.com/thumb/msid-123569554,imgsize-42956,width-400,resizemode-4/123569554.jpg" alt="What made ZigZag Vodka a global winner at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025" title="ZigZag Vodka, an Indian spirit, made a splash at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025, securing multiple silver and a bronze medal across its vodka variants. This achievement highlights the growing craftsmanship within India&#x27;s spirits industry and the global interest in innovative vodka expressions." decoding="async" fetchpriority="high"/></div></div></div><div class="cj2hz img_cptn"><span title="ZigZag Vodka, an Indian spirit, made a splash at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025, securing multiple silver and a bronze medal across its vodka variants. This achievement highlights the growing craftsmanship within India&#x27;s spirits industry and the global interest in innovative vodka expressions.">ZigZag Vodka, an Indian spirit, made a splash at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025, securing multiple silver and a bronze medal across its vodka variants. This achievement highlights the growing craftsmanship within India's spirits industry and the global interest in innovative vodka expressions.</span><div></div></div></section></div> </div></div>In a notable achievement for Indian spirits, ZigZag Vodka has garnered significant recognition at the Asia World Spirits Competition 2025, securing three silver medals and one bronze across its debut vodka variants.<!-- --> This marks a meaningful moment for Indian vodka on the international stage.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="3"></span>The competition, judged by seasoned industry experts, assessed a variety of spirits from across Asia and beyond, highlighting quality and craftsmanship. ZigZag’s success across its Original, Green Apple, Orange, and Lime vodkas reflects a carefully crafted product line that emphasizes distinctive ingredient choices and production techniques.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="6"></span>What sets ZigZag Vodka apart is its attention to the quality of ingredients and flavor profiles. Each variant is crafted using select botanicals and natural fruit essences that lend unique characteristics to the vodkas. For example, the Original vodka offers a smooth, clean palate that speaks to the brand’s focus on purity and refinement in distillation. The Green Apple and Orange variants incorporate natural fruit infusions, carefully balanced to deliver fresh, vibrant aromas and taste without overpowering the base spirit.<div data-type="in_view" class="  "><div class="js_tbl_2ad"></div><div class="mgid_second_mrec_parent"><div id="taboola-mid-article-thumbnails-123569554" class="wdt-taboola" data-target_type="mix" data-mode="thumbnails-mid" data-placement="Mid Article Thumbnails 1" data-pagetype="article" style="max-height:415px;overflow:hidden" data-ua-type="2" onclick="stpPgtn(event)"></div></div></div> and the Lime vodka brings a subtle citrus zing, achieved through the infusion of carefully sourced lime essence, providing a refreshing twist that complements the vodka’s crisp finish. These ingredients, combined with meticulous distillation processes, create vodkas that are both approachable and distinctive, appealing to a diverse range of palates.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="10"></span><div data-pos="0" class="id-r-component QbQNS undefined  
        "><div><img alt="2 (1060)" msid="123570020" width="" title="" placeholdersrc="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/83033472.cms" imgsize="23456" resizemode="4" offsetvertical="0" placeholdermsid="" type="thumb" src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/83033472.cms" class="" data-src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/imgsize-23456,msid-123570020,resizemode-4/2-1060.jpg" data-api-prerender="true"/></div></div><span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="12"></span>ZigZag’s recognition at the Asia World Spirits Competition underscores the growing craftsmanship within India&#x27;s spirits industry and the global interest in new, innovative expressions of vodka. <!-- -->The brand&#x27;s multi-medal haul reflects the potential for Indian vodkas to stand out in an increasingly competitive international market driven by quality, flavor complexity, and authenticity.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="16"></span>According to experts, ZigZag is officially the Indian vodka brand to win international honours across its entire range, and that too, within its very first year. It’s an honour to be recognised on a global stage, and it strengthens the belief in what they are building - a bold, design-led spirit from India that’s ready to be celebrated worldwide.”<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="19"></span>For the unversed, ZigZag is part of Saltborn, a visionary collective that aims to redefine premium consumer experiences with a focus on craftsmanship, authenticity, and innovation. Saltborn, founded by cousins Ishwaraj Singh Bhatia and his partner, started with Simba Beer and expanded into spirits like ZigZag Vodka. Saltborn’s ethos centers around bringing together artisanal dedication with forward-thinking design and creativity.<!-- --> This parent company’s support and vision have played a critical role in nurturing Simba’s growth and emergence onto the global stage.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="23"></span>As Indian craft spirits continue to evolve, ZigZag’s achievements highlight the importance of ingredient quality and flavor innovation—factors that are shaping the future of vodka appreciation worldwide. These accolades honor the use of genuine ingredients, a blend of traditional and innovative production methods, and a dedication to quality that appeals to both local and international audiences.<span class="id-r-component br" data-pos="25"></span><div class="cdatainfo modify_cdata_list_style id-r-component " data-pos="26"><br /></div></div><div class="js_tbl_readmore_btn" data-ua-type="1" onclick="stpPgtn(event)"></div></div><div class="authorComment  js_tblreadmore_hide"><div class="OtxlN" id="auhtor_widget"><div class="f2VrG"><div class="Mn6kH"><div data-pos="0" class="id-r-component QbQNS undefined  
        "><div><img alt="author" msid="" width="" title="" placeholdersrc="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/83033472.cms" imgsize="23456" resizemode="4" offsetvertical="0" placeholdermsid="" type="thumb" src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/83033472.cms" class="" data-src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/63379366.cms" data-api-prerender="true"/></div></div></div><div class="kgcOp"><div><h5>About the Author</h5><a href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/toireporter/author-toi-lifestyle-desk-479263437.cms" class="mMwSH" commonState="[object Object]" frmappuse="1">TOI Lifestyle Desk</a></div></div></div><div id="author_desc" class="GE1a7 oJgW0 "><p>The TOI Lifestyle Desk is a dynamic team of dedicated journalists who, with unwavering passion and commitment, sift through the pulse of the nation to curate a vibrant tapestry of lifestyle news for The Times of India readers.     var setCMPCookie = function(name, value, domainName, days){
        if(!!domainName){
            var domain = ";domain="+domainName;
        }
        if(!!days){
            //Below variable is one day time in mili seconds.
            var _oneDayinMS = 24*60*60*1000;
            var d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (days*_oneDayinMS));
            var expires = ";expires="+d.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name+"=" +value + ( ( expires ) ? expires : '' ) + ( ( domain ) ? domain : '' ) + ";path=/";
    };

                console.log('Failed to load gpt.js script');
            };
            document.head.appendChild(script);
        } else {
            attachGoogleCMPListners();
        }
    }
    
    function attachGoogleCMPListners() {
        window.googlefc.callbackQueue.push({
            'CONSENT_DATA_READY':
            () => __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2.2, (consentData, success) => {                    
                // 1. Check if GDPR applies
                if (consentData.gdprApplies === true) {
                    // 2. Check if the consent process was completed successfully
                    if (consentData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete' || consentData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded') {
                        // 3. Check if the user has consented to personalized ads (Purpose 1)
                        if (consentData.purpose && consentData.purpose.consents && consentData.purpose.consents["3"] === true) {
                            // User has consented to personalized ads, unset the opt out cookie
                            setOnAcceptOptOut();
                        } else {
                            // User did not consent to personalized ads, set the opt out cookie
                            setOnRejectOptOut();
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Consent process was not completed
                        setOnRejectOptOut();
                    }

                } else {
                    // GDPR doesn't apply, proceed with standard behavior or do not require consent
                    setOnAcceptOptOut();
                }
            })
        });

        // Queue the callback on the callbackQueue.
        window.googlefc.callbackQueue.push({
            'INITIAL_CCPA_DATA_READY':
            () => {
            switch (googlefc.ccpa.getInitialCcpaStatus()) {
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.CCPA_DOES_NOT_APPLY:
                setOnAcceptOptOut();
                break;
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.NOT_OPTED_OUT:
                setOnRejectOptOut();
                break;
                case googlefc.ccpa.InitialCcpaStatusEnum.OPTED_OUT:
                setOnAcceptOptOut();
                break;
            }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Call the function to ensure the script is loaded
    loadGPTScript();
} catch (err) {
  console.log("cmp_js error", err);

    TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager = (function() {
      /*
          1. Register overlay
          2. Decide overlay priority
          3. show overlay
  
  
          Register overlay
              - registerOverlay
                  - return onReadyCallback
                  - all popup's call onReadyCallback to mark status, they are ready to be called
              - read priority from config
              - create priority queue
  
          Decide overlay priority
              - read priority queue
              - call if 1st is ready
                      - if status OK  - call
                      - else if not needed to be called, call Next
              -
  
          Show overlay
              - save state in Localstorage
                  - show - true/false
                  - timestamp
  
  
          Config
              - popup list
              - priority for each
              - show frequency
      */
  
      const config = {
        browserStorageKey: 'popUpManagerHigherOrderPopUps',
      };
  
      const constants = {
        HRS_IN_DAY: 24,
        MINS_IN_HR: 60,
        SEC_IN_MIN: 60,
        MilliSEC_IN_SEC: 1000,
      };
  
      const fn = {
        _docReady(forcefully = false) {
          (function() {
            const referrer = document.referrer;
            try {
              if(forcefully) {

                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                if (data1.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(data1.actualData) &&
                  data1.actualData.length > 0 &&
                  (TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name] &&
                  TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name].getDetailsPopUp()?.id === 'interstitial')){
                    let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                    if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                        pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                    }
                    localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + data1.burninterval);
                    return;
                  }
              }
              if (window.localStorage && window.toi_client_side_settings) {
                  if(window.localStorage && localStorage.getItem("ccpaGdprPopupShown") === '1'){
                      let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                          if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                              pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                          }
                          localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + 1);
                      }
                let pageViews =
                  localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR') &&
                  parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                let data = JSON.parse(
                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                if (
                  data &&
                  Date.now() - data.time >
                  data.burntime * constants.SEC_IN_MIN * constants.MilliSEC_IN_SEC
                ) {
                  localStorage.removeItem(config.browserStorageKey);
                  localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', 1);
                  pageViews = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                  data = null;
                }
                if (!data) {
                  window.toi_client_side_settings.time = Date.now();
                  data = window.toi_client_side_settings;
                  data.actualData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data.priority));
                  data.actualData.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
                  if (!(localStorage.getItem("autoCcpaGdprPopupShown"))){
                    data.nextPageView = 1 + data.burninterval;
                  } else {
                    data.nextPageView = 1;
                  }
                  fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                }
                config.burninterval = data.burninterval;
                config.burntime = data.burntime;
                config.data = data;
                if (config.data.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(config.data.actualData) &&
                  config.data.actualData.length > 0) {
                  if(config.data.nextPageView - (config.burninterval + 1) === pageViews || forcefully){
                    if (!forcefully){
                      document.addEventListener('popup_manager_ready', function(event) {
                        if (!(TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name] && config.data.actualData[0].status === 1)) {
                          return fn._docReady(true);
                        }
                        TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                      });
                    } else {
                      if (!(TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name] && config.data.actualData[0].status === 1)) {
                        return fn._docReady(true);
                      }
                      TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                    }
                  }
                }

            } catch(ex){

        _saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews) {

            data.actualData.length > 0 && pageViews && pageViews > 0){
            // eslint-disable-next-line guard-for-in, no-restricted-syntax

                if (singleData.status === 1) {

                    if (shouldRepeat) {
                        singleData.priority = data.actualData[data.actualData.length - 1].priority + 1;
                        singleData.status = 0;
                        data.actualData.push(singleData);
                    }
                    data.actualData.shift();

                  singleData = data.actualData[0];
                  if (data.nextPageView === pageViews) {
                      singleData.status = 1;
                      data.nextPageView = pageViews + data.burninterval + 1;
                      return true;
                  }
                }
            });
            localStorage.setItem(config.browserStorageKey, JSON.stringify(data));
          }
        },
        _registerPopUp(id, callBack) {
          let callbacks = {};
          try{
            const popUp = fn._createPopUpObject(id, callBack);
            if (!popUp) return null;
            callbacks = {
              onReadyCallback: fn._onReadyCallback.bind(popUp),
              onShowCallback: fn._onShowCallback.bind(popUp),
              onUserActionCallback: popUp.onUserActionCallback,
              getDetail: fn._getDetails.bind(popUp),
            };
            popUp.callbacks = callbacks;
            TimesApps.PopUpList[id] = popUp;

              localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
            );
            let actualData = Array.isArray(data.actualData) && data.actualData.length > 0 ? data.actualData.map((d)=> d.name).sort() : [];

            if (actualData.join() === popupList.join()){
              document.dispatchEvent(TimesApps.popupManagerFullyInitilizedEvent);
            }
          } catch (err) {}

        },
        _getDetails(){
            return this.getDetailsPopUp();
        },
        _onReadyCallback(status) {
          this.onReadyCallback(status);
        },
        _onShowCallback(status) {
            /*
             * popup displayed
             */
            debugLogs('*** onShowCallback', this, status);
            this.onShowCallback(status);
            fn._setStatusInStorage(this, status);
          },
          _setStatusInStorage(obj, status) {
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();
            const index = fn._getIndex(data.actualData, obj.id);
            data.actualData[index].lastShownTimeStamp = Date.now();
            data.actualData[index].shown = status;

              fn._docReady(true);
            }
          },
          _getIndex(data, named) {
            let index = -1;
            if(data){
                Object.keys(data).forEach((key, i) => {
                    if (data[key].name === named) {
                        index = i;
                    }
                });
            }
            return index;
          },
        _createPopUpObject(id, showCallback = null) {
            const popUpdata = {};
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();

        },
        _isPopuManagerRunningInSession() {
          if (localStorage.getItem("pageViewsAfterGDPR") && fn._getStatusFromStorage()) return true;

        },
        _setStatusFromStorage(data) {

        _getStatusFromStorage() {
          const jsonData = localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey);

            data = JSON.parse(jsonData) || {};
          } catch (e) {
            data = null;
            //console.log('popupManager, JSON error');
          }

          return data;
        },
      };

      fn._docReady();
      const regiteredPopup = window.TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager.cmd || [];
      setTimeout(()=>{
        fn._init();
      },100)

      const api = {
        cmd: {
            push: function(callback){
                if(typeof callback === 'function'){
                    callback();
                }
            }
        },
        regiteredPopup: regiteredPopup,
        register(id, showCallback) {
          return fn._registerPopUp(id, showCallback);
        },
        isPopuMangerRunning() {
          return fn._isPopuManagerRunningInSession();
        },
        reloadPopupManager(forcefully) {
          return fn._docReady(forcefully);
        },
      };

      return api;
    })();

function getCookie(cname) {
  var name = cname + '=';
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return '';
}

function handleInterstitial(tmpl) {
  var ref = document.referrer;
  document.cookie="ns=1";
  //In incognito mode, first time there is no cookie and user won't get interstitial, so setting a cookie
  // so that it doesn't return first time in incognito
  //window.location.host.match(/toispadev/) ||
  //(ref.indexOf('google') > -1) ||

  if (
    window.nsShowMaxCount < 1 ||
    window.isPrime ||
    (ref.match(/defaultinterstitial/) && getCookie('nsIstial')) ||
    (ref.match(/defaultinterstitial_indirect/) && getCookie('nsIstial')) ||
    document.cookie === '' ||
    /bot|googlebot|crawler|spider|robot|crawling/i.test(navigator.userAgent)
  ) {
    //toiprops.cookie.remove('nsIstial');
    document.cookie = 'nsIstial=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; domain=.indiatimes.com';
    return true;
  }

  var intCookieName = tmpl ? 'nsIstial_Cook_Adex' : 'nsIstial_Cook';
  var goToInterstitialPage = function() {
    var queryParams = window.location.search;
    if(queryParams.indexOf('back=1') == -1){
      var backto = window.location.pathname + queryParams;
      var template = window.location.pathname === '/us'? 'defaultinterstitial_int_us': 'defaultinterstitial';
      template = tmpl || template;
      window.location.replace(
        'https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/' + template + '.cms?b=' + backto
      );
    }
  };
  var getCookieExpireDate = function() {
    var expireAfter = tmpl ? 0.5 : 1;
    var currentDate = new Date();
    var expirationTime = new Date(currentDate.getTime() +  expireAfter * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    var expirationTimeString = expirationTime.toUTCString();
    return "; expires=" + expirationTimeString + "; path=/";
  }
  var cookieExpire = 1 || tmpl ? getCookieExpireDate() : ''
  ;

  var nsShownCount = parseInt(getCookie(intCookieName), 10) || 0;

  // if use has been in the same session and refreshed the page more than 10 times
  // reset the flags
  if (nsShownCount > 10) {
    document.cookie = intCookieName + '=null';
    nsShownCount = 0;
  }

  if (nsShownCount < window.nsShowMaxCount) {
    if (
      !(
        window.location.href.indexOf('order_id') > -1 &&
        localStorage.getItem('toi_subscription')
      )
    ) {
      nsShownCount += 1;
      document.cookie = intCookieName + '=' + nsShownCount + cookieExpire;
      goToInterstitialPage();
    }
  }
  else{
    nsShownCount += 1;
    document.cookie = intCookieName + '=' + nsShownCount + cookieExpire;
  }

  return;
}
function initiateWInterstitial(tmpl){

  if (
    window.nsShowMaxCount > 0 &&
    !window.location.href.match(/TOI_browsernotification/)
  ) {
    handleInterstitial(tmpl);
  }
}

    function detectAdBlock(callback) {
      // Wait for DOM ready
      if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
          detectAdBlock(callback);
        });
        return;
      }
    
      // Create a bait element with common ad-related class names
      var bait = document.createElement('div');
      bait.className = 'ads ad adsbox ad-banner ad-placement ad-unit ad-container sponsored';
      bait.style.cssText = 'width: 1px; height: 1px; position: absolute; left: -999px;';
      document.body.appendChild(bait);
    
      // Allow time for ad blocker to act
      setTimeout(function () {
        var isBlocked = false;
    
        if (!bait || bait.offsetParent === null || bait.offsetHeight === 0 || bait.clientHeight === 0) {
          isBlocked = true;
        }
    
        document.body.removeChild(bait);
        callback(isBlocked);
      }, 200); // 100–300ms is usually safe
    }
    window.DisplayBlkrDetected = function(type) {
      _adShieldObj.log('DisplayBlkrDetected called with type: ' + type);
      window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled = _adShieldObj.getCookie('displayRender')
        ? _adShieldObj.getCookie('displayRender')
        : null;
      _adShieldObj.log('displayBlkrEnabled set to: ' + window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled);
      if (type === 'prebidBlocked') {
        window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled = 0;

The Green Apple and Orange variants incorporate natural fruit infusions, carefully balanced to deliver fresh, vibrant aromas and taste without overpowering the base spirit. and the Lime vodka brings a subtle citrus zing, achieved through the infusion of carefully sourced lime essence, providing a refreshing twist that complements the vodka’s crisp finish. These ingredients, combined with meticulous distillation processes, create vodkas that are both approachable and distinctive, appealing to a diverse range of palates.ZigZag’s recognition at the Asia World Spirits Competition underscores the growing craftsmanship within India's spirits industry and the global interest in new, innovative expressions of vodka. The brand's multi-medal haul reflects the potential for Indian vodkas to stand out in an increasingly competitive international market driven by quality, flavor complexity, and authenticity.According to experts, ZigZag is officially the Indian vodka brand to win international honours across its entire range, and that too, within its very first year. It’s an honour to be recognised on a global stage, and it strengthens the belief in what they are building - a bold, design-led spirit from India that’s ready to be celebrated worldwide.”For the unversed, ZigZag is part of Saltborn, a visionary collective that aims to redefine premium consumer experiences with a focus on craftsmanship, authenticity, and innovation. Saltborn, founded by cousins Ishwaraj Singh Bhatia and his partner, started with Simba Beer and expanded into spirits like ZigZag Vodka. Saltborn’s ethos centers around bringing together artisanal dedication with forward-thinking design and creativity. This parent company’s support and vision have played a critical role in nurturing Simba’s growth and emergence onto the global stage.As Indian craft spirits continue to evolve, ZigZag’s achievements highlight the importance of ingredient quality and flavor innovation—factors that are shaping the future of vodka appreciation worldwide. These accolades honor the use of genuine ingredients, a blend of traditional and innovative production methods, and a dedication to quality that appeals to both local and international
